\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{/* The symbols declared in this file (including the functions declared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{ * as extern) are PRIVATE.  They are not part of the libpng public}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{ * interface, and are not recommended for use by regular applications.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{ * Some of them may become public in the future; others may stay private,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{ * change in an incompatible way, or even disappear.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{ * Although the libpng users are not forbidden to include this header,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{ * they should be well aware of the issues that may arise from doing so.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{/* Feature Test Macros.  The following are defined here to ensure that correctly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{ * implemented libraries reveal the APIs libpng needs to build and hide those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{ * that are not needed and potentially damaging to the compilation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{ * Feature Test Macros must be defined before any system header is included (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{ * POSIX 1003.1 2.8.2 "{}POSIX Symbols."{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{ * These macros only have an effect if the operating system supports either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{ * POSIX 1003.1 or C99, or both.  On other operating systems (particularly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{ * Windows/Visual Studio) there is no effect; the OS specific tests below are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{ * still required (as of 2011-\/05-\/02.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef \_POSIX\_SOURCE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# define \_POSIX\_SOURCE 1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* Just the POSIX 1003.1 and C89 APIs */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 }
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_VERSION\_INFO\_ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{/* Standard library headers not required by png.h: */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{44 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  include <stdlib.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{45 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  include <string.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{46 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNGLIB\_BUILD }\textcolor{comment}{/*libpng is being built, not used*/}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 }
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{/* If HAVE\_CONFIG\_H is defined during the build then the build system must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{ * provide an appropriate "{}config.h"{} file on the include path.  The header file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{comment}{ * must provide definitions as required below (search for "{}HAVE\_CONFIG\_H"{});}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 \textcolor{comment}{ * see configure.ac for more details of the requirements.  The macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}PNG\_NO\_CONFIG\_H"{} is provided for maintainers to test for dependencies on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \textcolor{comment}{ * 'configure'; define this macro to prevent the configure build including the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 \textcolor{comment}{ * configure generated config.h.  Libpng is expected to compile without *any*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57 \textcolor{comment}{ * special build system support on a reasonably ANSI-\/C compliant system.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(HAVE\_CONFIG\_H) \&\& !defined(PNG\_NO\_CONFIG\_H)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  include <config.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 }
\DoxyCodeLine{62    \textcolor{comment}{/* Pick up the definition of 'restrict' from config.h if it was read: */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_RESTRICT restrict}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{90 }
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{/* Compile time options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{ * =====================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{ * In a multi-\/arch build the compiler may compile the code several times for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{ * same object module, producing different binaries for different architectures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{ * When this happens configure-\/time setting of the target host options cannot be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{ * done and this interferes with the handling of the ARM NEON optimizations, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{ * possibly other similar optimizations.  Put additional tests here; in general}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{ * this is needed when the same option can be changed at both compile time and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{ * run time depending on the target OS (i.e. iOS vs Android.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: symbol prefixing does not pass \$(CFLAGS) to the preprocessor, because}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{ * this is not possible with certain compilers (Oracle SUN OS CC), as a result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is necessary to ensure that all extern functions that *might* be used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{ * regardless of \$(CFLAGS) get declared in this file.  The test on \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{ * below is one example of this behavior because it is controlled by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{ * presence or not of -\/mfpu=neon on the GCC command line, it is possible to do}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{ * this in \$(CC), e.g. "{}CC=gcc -\/mfpu=neon"{}, but people who build libpng rarely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{ * do this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111    \textcolor{comment}{/* ARM NEON optimizations are being controlled by the compiler settings,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{    * typically the target FPU.  If the FPU has been set to NEON (-\/mfpu=neon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{    * with GCC) then the compiler will define \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_ and we can rely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{    * unconditionally on NEON instructions not crashing, otherwise we must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{    * disable use of NEON instructions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{    * NOTE: at present these optimizations depend on 'ALIGNED\_MEMORY', so they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{    * can only be turned on automatically if that is supported too.  If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{    * PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT is set in CPPFLAGS (to >0) then arm/arm\_init.c will fail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{    * to compile with an appropriate \#error if ALIGNED\_MEMORY has been turned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{    * off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{    * Note that gcc-\/4.9 defines \_\_ARM\_NEON instead of the deprecated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{    * \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_, so we check both variants.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{    * To disable ARM\_NEON optimizations entirely, and skip compiling the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{    * associated assembler code, pass -\/-\/enable-\/arm-\/neon=no to configure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{    * or put -\/DPNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT=0 in CPPFLAGS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  if (defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_) || defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON)) \&\& \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   defined(PNG\_ALIGNED\_MEMORY\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 }
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT > 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139    \textcolor{comment}{/* NEON optimizations are to be at least considered by libpng, so enable the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{    * callbacks to do this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_FILTER\_OPTIMIZATIONS png\_init\_filter\_functions\_neon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 }
\DoxyCodeLine{144    \textcolor{comment}{/* By default the 'intrinsics' code in arm/filter\_neon\_intrinsics.c is used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{    * if possible -\/ if \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_ is set and the compiler version is not known}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{    * to be broken.  This is controlled by PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION which can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{    * be:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{    *    1  The intrinsics code (the default with \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{    *    2  The hand coded assembler (the default without \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{    *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{    * It is possible to set PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION in CPPFLAGS, however}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{    * this is *NOT* supported and may cease to work even after a minor revision}}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{    * to libpng.  It *is* valid to do this for testing purposes, e.g. speed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{    * testing or a new compiler, but the results should be communicated to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{    * libpng implementation list for incorporation in the next minor release.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  ifndef PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     if defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_) || defined(\_\_ARM\_NEON)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        if defined(\_\_clang\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{161             \textcolor{comment}{/* At present it is unknown by the libpng developers which versions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{162 \textcolor{comment}{             * of clang support the intrinsics, however some or perhaps all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{             * versions do not work with the assembler so this may be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{             * irrelevant, so just use the default (do nothing here.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{166 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        elif defined(\_\_GNUC\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{167             \textcolor{comment}{/* GCC 4.5.4 NEON support is known to be broken.  4.6.3 is known to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{168 \textcolor{comment}{             * work, so if this *is* GCC, or G++, look for a version >4.5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{169 \textcolor{comment}{             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{170 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#           if \_\_GNUC\_\_ < 4 || (\_\_GNUC\_\_ == 4 \&\& \_\_GNUC\_MINOR\_\_ < 6)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{171 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#              define PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{172 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#           endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* no GNUC support */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{173 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* \_\_GNUC\_\_ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{174 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     else }\textcolor{comment}{/* !defined \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{175          \textcolor{comment}{/* The 'intrinsics' code simply won't compile without this -\/mfpu=neon:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{176 \textcolor{comment}{          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{177 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        if !defined(\_\_aarch64\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{178             \textcolor{comment}{/* The assembler code currently does not work on ARM64 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{179 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#          define PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{180 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* \_\_aarch64\_\_ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{181 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* \_\_ARM\_NEON\_\_ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{182 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* !PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{183 }
\DoxyCodeLine{184 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  ifndef PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{185       \textcolor{comment}{/* Use the intrinsics code by default. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{186 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_IMPLEMENTATION 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{187 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{188 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_ARM\_NEON\_OPT > 0 */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{190 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_MIPS\_MSA\_OPT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{191 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  if defined(\_\_mips\_msa) \&\& (\_\_mips\_isa\_rev >= 5) \&\& defined(PNG\_ALIGNED\_MEMORY\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{192 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_MIPS\_MSA\_OPT 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{193 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{194 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_MIPS\_MSA\_OPT 0}}

\DoxyCodeLine{197 }

\DoxyCodeLine{199 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  if defined(\_\_PPC64\_\_) \&\& defined(\_\_ALTIVEC\_\_) \&\& defined(\_\_VSX\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{200 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_POWERPC\_VSX\_OPT 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{201 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{202 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define PNG\_POWERPC\_VSX\_OPT 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{203 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{204 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{205 }
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_OPT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   ifdef PNG\_INTEL\_SSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208       \textcolor{comment}{/* Only check for SSE if the build configuration has been modified to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{comment}{       * enable SSE optimizations.  This means that these optimizations will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{comment}{       * be off by default.  See contrib/intel for more details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{comment}{       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     if defined(\_\_SSE4\_1\_\_) || defined(\_\_AVX\_\_) || defined(\_\_SSSE3\_\_) || \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) || defined(\_M\_X64) || defined(\_M\_AMD64) || \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (defined(\_M\_IX86\_FP) \&\& \_M\_IX86\_FP >= 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_OPT 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{216 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_OPT 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{220 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_OPT 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{221 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{222 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{223 }
\DoxyCodeLine{224 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_OPT > 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{225 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   ifndef PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{226 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      if defined(\_\_SSE4\_1\_\_) || defined(\_\_AVX\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{227           \textcolor{comment}{/* We are not actually using AVX, but checking for AVX is the best}}
\DoxyCodeLine{228 \textcolor{comment}{             way we can detect SSE4.1 and SSSE3 on MSVC.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{229 \textcolor{comment}{          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{230 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION 3}}
\DoxyCodeLine{231 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      elif defined(\_\_SSSE3\_\_)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{232 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{233 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      elif defined(\_\_SSE2\_\_) || defined(\_M\_X64) || defined(\_M\_AMD64) || \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{preprocessor}{       (defined(\_M\_IX86\_FP) \&\& \_M\_IX86\_FP >= 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#         define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{238 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{239 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{240 }
\DoxyCodeLine{241 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   if PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION > 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{242 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#      define PNG\_FILTER\_OPTIMIZATIONS png\_init\_filter\_functions\_sse2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#   define PNG\_INTEL\_SSE\_IMPLEMENTATION 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{256 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#           endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* no GNUC support */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{274 \textcolor{comment}{/* Is this a build of a DLL where compilation of the object modules requires}}
\DoxyCodeLine{275 \textcolor{comment}{ * different preprocessor settings to those required for a simple library?  If}}
\DoxyCodeLine{276 \textcolor{comment}{ * so PNG\_BUILD\_DLL must be set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{277 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{278 \textcolor{comment}{ * If libpng is used inside a DLL but that DLL does not export the libpng APIs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{279 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_BUILD\_DLL must not be set.  To avoid the code below kicking in build a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{280 \textcolor{comment}{ * static library of libpng then link the DLL against that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{281 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{393 \textcolor{comment}{/* This is a global switch to set the compilation for an installed system}}
\DoxyCodeLine{394 \textcolor{comment}{ * (a release build).  It can be set for testing debug builds to ensure that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{395 \textcolor{comment}{ * they will compile when the build type is switched to RC or STABLE, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{396 \textcolor{comment}{ * default is just to use PNG\_LIBPNG\_BUILD\_BASE\_TYPE.  Set this in CPPFLAGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{397 \textcolor{comment}{ * with either:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{398 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{399 \textcolor{comment}{ *   -\/DPNG\_RELEASE\_BUILD Turns on the release compile path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{400 \textcolor{comment}{ *   -\/DPNG\_RELEASE\_BUILD=0 Turns it off}}
\DoxyCodeLine{401 \textcolor{comment}{ * or in your pngusr.h with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{402 \textcolor{comment}{ *   \#define PNG\_RELEASE\_BUILD=1 Turns on the release compile path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{403 \textcolor{comment}{ *   \#define PNG\_RELEASE\_BUILD=0 Turns it off}}
\DoxyCodeLine{404 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{405 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_RELEASE\_BUILD}}

\DoxyCodeLine{408 }
\DoxyCodeLine{409 \textcolor{comment}{/* SECURITY and SAFETY:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{410 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{411 \textcolor{comment}{ * libpng is built with support for internal limits on image dimensions and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{412 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory usage.  These are documented in scripts/pnglibconf.dfa of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{413 \textcolor{comment}{ * source and recorded in the machine generated header file pnglibconf.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{414 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{415 }
\DoxyCodeLine{416 \textcolor{comment}{/* If you are running on a machine where you cannot allocate more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{417 \textcolor{comment}{ * than 64K of memory at once, uncomment this.  While libpng will not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{418 \textcolor{comment}{ * normally need that much memory in a chunk (unless you load up a very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{419 \textcolor{comment}{ * large file), zlib needs to know how big of a chunk it can use, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{420 \textcolor{comment}{ * libpng thus makes sure to check any memory allocation to verify it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{421 \textcolor{comment}{ * will fit into memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{422 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{423 \textcolor{comment}{ * zlib provides 'MAXSEG\_64K' which, if defined, indicates the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{424 \textcolor{comment}{ * same limit and pngconf.h (already included) sets the limit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{425 \textcolor{comment}{ * if certain operating systems are detected.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{426 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{427 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(MAXSEG\_64K) \&\& !defined(PNG\_MAX\_MALLOC\_64K)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{428 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_MAX\_MALLOC\_64K}}
\DoxyCodeLine{429 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{430 }
\DoxyCodeLine{431 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_UNUSED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{432 \textcolor{comment}{/* Unused formal parameter warnings are silenced using the following macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{433 \textcolor{comment}{ * which is expected to have no bad effects on performance (optimizing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{434 \textcolor{comment}{ * compilers will probably remove it entirely).  Note that if you replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{435 \textcolor{comment}{ * it with something other than whitespace, you must include the terminating}}
\DoxyCodeLine{436 \textcolor{comment}{ * semicolon.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{437 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{438 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_UNUSED(param) (void)param;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{439 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{440 }
\DoxyCodeLine{441 \textcolor{comment}{/* Just a little check that someone hasn't tried to define something}}

\DoxyCodeLine{443 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{444 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if (PNG\_ZBUF\_SIZE > 65536L) \&\& defined(PNG\_MAX\_MALLOC\_64K)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{480 }
\DoxyCodeLine{481 \textcolor{comment}{/* C allows up-\/casts from (void*) to any pointer and (const void*) to any}}
\DoxyCodeLine{482 \textcolor{comment}{ * pointer to a const object.  C++ regards this as a type error and requires an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{483 \textcolor{comment}{ * explicit, static, cast and provides the static\_cast<> rune to ensure that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{484 \textcolor{comment}{ * const is not cast away.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{485 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{486 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef \_\_cplusplus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{487 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_voidcast(type, value) static\_cast<type>(value)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{488 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_constcast(type, value) const\_cast<type>(value)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{489 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_aligncast(type, value) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{490 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   static\_cast<type>(static\_cast<void*>(value))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{491 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_aligncastconst(type, value) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{492 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   static\_cast<type>(static\_cast<const void*>(value))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{493 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{494 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_voidcast(type, value) (value)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{495 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  ifdef \_WIN64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{496 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     ifdef \_\_GNUC\_\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{497          \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ac99f817787241d68ceb93f9aafef297b}{png\_ptruint}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{498 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{499          \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \_\_int64 \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ac99f817787241d68ceb93f9aafef297b}{png\_ptruint}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{500 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{501 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{502       \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ac99f817787241d68ceb93f9aafef297b}{png\_ptruint}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{503 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{570 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_ALIGN\_OFFSET 2 }\textcolor{comment}{/* use offsetof to determine alignment */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{571 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{572 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_ALIGN\_OFFSET -\/1 }\textcolor{comment}{/* prevent the use of this */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{573 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{574 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ALIGN\_SIZE   3 }\textcolor{comment}{/* use sizeof to determine alignment */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{575 }
\DoxyCodeLine{576 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_ALIGN\_TYPE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{577    \textcolor{comment}{/* Default to using aligned access optimizations and requiring alignment to a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{578 \textcolor{comment}{    * multiple of the data type size.  Override in a compiler specific fashion}}
\DoxyCodeLine{579 \textcolor{comment}{    * if necessary by inserting tests here:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{580 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{581 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_ALIGN\_TYPE PNG\_ALIGN\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{582 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{583 }
\DoxyCodeLine{584 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if PNG\_ALIGN\_TYPE == PNG\_ALIGN\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{585    \textcolor{comment}{/* This is used because in some compiler implementations non-\/aligned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{586 \textcolor{comment}{    * structure members are supported, so the offsetof approach below fails.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{587 \textcolor{comment}{    * Set PNG\_ALIGN\_SIZE=0 for compiler combinations where unaligned access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{588 \textcolor{comment}{    * is good for performance.  Do not do this unless you have tested the result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{589 \textcolor{comment}{    * and understand it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{590 \textcolor{comment}{    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{591 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_alignof(type) (sizeof (type))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{592 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{593 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  if PNG\_ALIGN\_TYPE == PNG\_ALIGN\_OFFSET}}
\DoxyCodeLine{594 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     define png\_alignof(type) offsetof(struct\{char c; type t;\}, t)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{595 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{596 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     if PNG\_ALIGN\_TYPE == PNG\_ALIGN\_ALWAYS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{597 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#        define png\_alignof(type) (1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{598 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#     endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{599       \textcolor{comment}{/* Else leave png\_alignof undefined to prevent use thereof */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{600 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{601 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{602 }
\DoxyCodeLine{603 \textcolor{comment}{/* This implicitly assumes alignment is always to a power of 2. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{604 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef png\_alignof}}
\DoxyCodeLine{605 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_isaligned(ptr, type)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{606 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (((type)((const char*)ptr-\/(const char*)0) \& \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{607 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (type)(png\_alignof(type)-\/1)) == 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{608 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{609 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define png\_isaligned(ptr, type) 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{610 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{611 }
\DoxyCodeLine{612 \textcolor{comment}{/* End of memory model/platform independent support */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{613 \textcolor{comment}{/* End of 1.5.0beta36 move from pngconf.h */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{720 \textcolor{comment}{/* Save typing and make code easier to understand */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721 }
\DoxyCodeLine{722 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_COLOR\_DIST(c1, c2) (abs((int)((c1).red) -\/ (int)((c2).red)) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   abs((int)((c1).green) -\/ (int)((c2).green)) + \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   abs((int)((c1).blue) -\/ (int)((c2).blue)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725 }
\DoxyCodeLine{726 \textcolor{comment}{/* Added to libpng-\/1.6.0: scale a 16-\/bit value in the range 0..65535 to 0..255}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727 \textcolor{comment}{ * by dividing by 257 *with rounding*.  This macro is exact for the given range.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728 \textcolor{comment}{ * See the discourse in pngrtran.c png\_do\_scale\_16\_to\_8.  The values in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729 \textcolor{comment}{ * macro were established by experiment (modifying the added value).  The macro}}
\DoxyCodeLine{730 \textcolor{comment}{ * has a second variant that takes a value already scaled by 255 and divides by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{731 \textcolor{comment}{ * 65535 -\/ this has a maximum error of .502.  Over the range 0..65535*65535 it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{732 \textcolor{comment}{ * only gives off-\/by-\/one errors and only for 0.5\% (1 in 200) of the values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{733 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{734 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_DIV65535(v24) (((v24) + 32895) >> 16)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{735 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_DIV257(v16) PNG\_DIV65535((png\_uint\_32)(v16) * 255)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{736 }
\DoxyCodeLine{737 \textcolor{comment}{/* Added to libpng-\/1.2.6 JB */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{738 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_ROWBYTES(pixel\_bits, width) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{739 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((pixel\_bits) >= 8 ? \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{740 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((size\_t)(width) * (((size\_t)(pixel\_bits)) >> 3)) : \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{741 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    (( ((size\_t)(width) * ((size\_t)(pixel\_bits))) + 7) >> 3) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{742 }
\DoxyCodeLine{743 \textcolor{comment}{/* This returns the number of trailing bits in the last byte of a row, 0 if the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{744 \textcolor{comment}{ * last byte is completely full of pixels.  It is, in principle, (pixel\_bits x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{745 \textcolor{comment}{ * width) \% 8, but that would overflow for large 'width'.  The second macro is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{746 \textcolor{comment}{ * the same except that it returns the number of unused bits in the last byte;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{747 \textcolor{comment}{ * (8-\/TRAILBITS), but 0 when TRAILBITS is 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{748 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{749 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: these macros are intended to be self-\/evidently correct and never}}
\DoxyCodeLine{750 \textcolor{comment}{ * overflow on the assumption that pixel\_bits is in the range 0..255.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{751 \textcolor{comment}{ * arguments are evaluated only once and they can be signed (e.g. as a result of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{752 \textcolor{comment}{ * the integral promotions).  The result of the expression always has type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{753 \textcolor{comment}{ * (png\_uint\_32), however the compiler always knows it is in the range 0..7.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{754 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{755 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_TRAILBITS(pixel\_bits, width) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{756 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    (((pixel\_bits) * ((width) \% (png\_uint\_32)8)) \% 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{757 }
\DoxyCodeLine{758 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_PADBITS(pixel\_bits, width) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{759 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((8 -\/ PNG\_TRAILBITS(pixel\_bits, width)) \% 8)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{761 \textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_OUT\_OF\_RANGE returns true if value is outside the range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{762 \textcolor{comment}{ * ideal-\/delta..ideal+delta.  Each argument is evaluated twice.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{763 \textcolor{comment}{ * "{}ideal"{} and "{}delta"{} should be constants, normally simple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{764 \textcolor{comment}{ * integers, "{}value"{} a variable. Added to libpng-\/1.2.6 JB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{765 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{766 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_OUT\_OF\_RANGE(value, ideal, delta) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{767 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ( (value) < (ideal)-\/(delta) || (value) > (ideal)+(delta) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{768 }
\DoxyCodeLine{769 \textcolor{comment}{/* Conversions between fixed and floating point, only defined if}}
\DoxyCodeLine{770 \textcolor{comment}{ * required (to make sure the code doesn't accidentally use float}}
\DoxyCodeLine{771 \textcolor{comment}{ * when it is supposedly disabled.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{772 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{773 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FLOATING\_POINT\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{774 \textcolor{comment}{/* The floating point conversion can't overflow, though it can and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{775 \textcolor{comment}{ * does lose accuracy relative to the original fixed point value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{776 \textcolor{comment}{ * In practice this doesn't matter because png\_fixed\_point only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{777 \textcolor{comment}{ * stores numbers with very low precision.  The png\_ptr and s}}
\DoxyCodeLine{778 \textcolor{comment}{ * arguments are unused by default but are there in case error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{779 \textcolor{comment}{ * checking becomes a requirement.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{780 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{781 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_float(png\_ptr, fixed, s) (.00001 * (fixed))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{782 }
\DoxyCodeLine{783 \textcolor{comment}{/* The fixed point conversion performs range checking and evaluates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{784 \textcolor{comment}{ * its argument multiple times, so must be used with care.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{785 \textcolor{comment}{ * range checking uses the PNG specification values for a signed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{786 \textcolor{comment}{ * 32-\/bit fixed point value except that the values are deliberately}}
\DoxyCodeLine{787 \textcolor{comment}{ * rounded-\/to-\/zero to an integral value -\/ 21474 (21474.83 is roughly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{788 \textcolor{comment}{ * (2\string^31-\/1) * 100000). 's' is a string that describes the value being}}
\DoxyCodeLine{789 \textcolor{comment}{ * converted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{790 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{791 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: this macro will raise a png\_error if the range check fails,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{792 \textcolor{comment}{ * therefore it is normally only appropriate to use this on values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793 \textcolor{comment}{ * that come from API calls or other sources where an out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794 \textcolor{comment}{ * error indicates a programming error, not a data error!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: by default this is off -\/ the macro is not used -\/ because the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797 \textcolor{comment}{ * function call saves a lot of code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{799 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FIXED\_POINT\_MACRO\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{800 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_fixed(png\_ptr, fp, s) ((fp) <= 21474 \&\& (fp) >= -\/21474 ?\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{801 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    ((png\_fixed\_point)(100000 * (fp))) : (png\_fixed\_error(png\_ptr, s),0))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{803 \textcolor{comment}{/* else the corresponding function is defined below, inside the scope of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{804 \textcolor{comment}{ * cplusplus test.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{805 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{806 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{807 }
\DoxyCodeLine{808 \textcolor{comment}{/* Constants for known chunk types.  If you need to add a chunk, define the name}}
\DoxyCodeLine{809 \textcolor{comment}{ * here.  For historical reasons these constants have the form png\_<name>; i.e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{810 \textcolor{comment}{ * the prefix is lower case.  Please use decimal values as the parameters to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{811 \textcolor{comment}{ * match the ISO PNG specification and to avoid relying on the C locale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{812 \textcolor{comment}{ * interpretation of character values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{813 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{814 \textcolor{comment}{ * Prior to 1.5.6 these constants were strings, as of 1.5.6 png\_uint\_32 values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{815 \textcolor{comment}{ * are computed and a new macro (PNG\_STRING\_FROM\_CHUNK) added to allow a string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{816 \textcolor{comment}{ * to be generated if required.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{817 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{818 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_32b correctly produces a value shifted by up to 24 bits, even on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{819 \textcolor{comment}{ * architectures where (int) is only 16 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{820 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{821 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_32b(b,s) ((png\_uint\_32)(b) << (s))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{822 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_U32(b1,b2,b3,b4) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{823 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (PNG\_32b(b1,24) | PNG\_32b(b2,16) | PNG\_32b(b3,8) | PNG\_32b(b4,0))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{824 }
\DoxyCodeLine{825 \textcolor{comment}{/* Constants for known chunk types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{826 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{827 \textcolor{comment}{ * MAINTAINERS: If you need to add a chunk, define the name here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{828 \textcolor{comment}{ * For historical reasons these constants have the form png\_<name>; i.e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{829 \textcolor{comment}{ * the prefix is lower case.  Please use decimal values as the parameters to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{830 \textcolor{comment}{ * match the ISO PNG specification and to avoid relying on the C locale}}
\DoxyCodeLine{831 \textcolor{comment}{ * interpretation of character values.  Please keep the list sorted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{832 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{833 \textcolor{comment}{ * Notice that PNG\_U32 is used to define a 32-\/bit value for the 4 byte chunk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{834 \textcolor{comment}{ * type.  In fact the specification does not express chunk types this way,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{835 \textcolor{comment}{ * however using a 32-\/bit value means that the chunk type can be read from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{836 \textcolor{comment}{ * stream using exactly the same code as used for a 32-\/bit unsigned value and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{837 \textcolor{comment}{ * can be examined far more efficiently (using one arithmetic compare).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{838 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{839 \textcolor{comment}{ * Prior to 1.5.6 the chunk type constants were expressed as C strings.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{840 \textcolor{comment}{ * libpng API still uses strings for 'unknown' chunks and a macro,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{841 \textcolor{comment}{ * PNG\_STRING\_FROM\_CHUNK, allows a string to be generated if required.  Notice}}
\DoxyCodeLine{842 \textcolor{comment}{ * that for portable code numeric values must still be used; the string "{}IHDR"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{843 \textcolor{comment}{ * is not portable and neither is PNG\_U32('I', 'H', 'D', 'R').}}
\DoxyCodeLine{844 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{845 \textcolor{comment}{ * In 1.7.0 the definitions will be made public in png.h to avoid having to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{846 \textcolor{comment}{ * duplicate the same definitions in application code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{847 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{848 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_IDAT PNG\_U32( 73,  68,  65,  84)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{849 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_IEND PNG\_U32( 73,  69,  78,  68)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{850 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_IHDR PNG\_U32( 73,  72,  68,  82)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{851 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_PLTE PNG\_U32( 80,  76,  84,  69)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{852 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_bKGD PNG\_U32( 98,  75,  71,  68)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{853 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_cHRM PNG\_U32( 99,  72,  82,  77)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{854 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_eXIf PNG\_U32(101,  88,  73, 102) }\textcolor{comment}{/* registered July 2017 */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{855 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_fRAc PNG\_U32(102,  82,  65,  99) }\textcolor{comment}{/* registered, not defined */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{856 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_gAMA PNG\_U32(103,  65,  77,  65)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{857 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_gIFg PNG\_U32(103,  73,  70, 103)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{858 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define png\_gIFt PNG\_U32(103,  73,  70, 116) }\textcolor{comment}{/* deprecated */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{875 }
\DoxyCodeLine{876 \textcolor{comment}{/* The following will work on (signed char*) strings, whereas the get\_uint\_32}}
\DoxyCodeLine{877 \textcolor{comment}{ * macro will fail on top-\/bit-\/set values because of the sign extension.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{878 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{879 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CHUNK\_FROM\_STRING(s)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{880 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   PNG\_U32(0xff \& (s)[0], 0xff \& (s)[1], 0xff \& (s)[2], 0xff \& (s)[3])}}
\DoxyCodeLine{881 }
\DoxyCodeLine{882 \textcolor{comment}{/* This uses (char), not (png\_byte) to avoid warnings on systems where (char) is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{883 \textcolor{comment}{ * signed and the argument is a (char[])  This macro will fail miserably on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{884 \textcolor{comment}{ * systems where (char) is more than 8 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{885 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{886 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_STRING\_FROM\_CHUNK(s,c)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{887 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (void)(((char*)(s))[0]=(char)(((c)>>24) \& 0xff), \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{888 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((char*)(s))[1]=(char)(((c)>>16) \& 0xff),\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{889 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((char*)(s))[2]=(char)(((c)>>8) \& 0xff), \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{890 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   ((char*)(s))[3]=(char)((c \& 0xff)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{891 }
\DoxyCodeLine{892 \textcolor{comment}{/* Do the same but terminate with a null character. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{893 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CSTRING\_FROM\_CHUNK(s,c)\(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{894 \textcolor{preprocessor}{   (void)(PNG\_STRING\_FROM\_CHUNK(s,c), ((char*)(s))[4] = 0)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{895 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1029 \textcolor{comment}{/* Magic to create a struct when there is no struct to call the user supplied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1030 \textcolor{comment}{ * memory allocators.  Because error handling has not been set up the memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1031 \textcolor{comment}{ * handlers can't safely call png\_error, but this is an obscure and undocumented}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1032 \textcolor{comment}{ * restriction so libpng has to assume that the 'free' handler, at least, might}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1249 \textcolor{comment}{/* Combine a row of data, dealing with alpha, etc. if requested.  'row' is an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1250 \textcolor{comment}{ * array of png\_ptr-\/>width pixels.  If the image is not interlaced or this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1251 \textcolor{comment}{ * is the final pass this just does a memcpy, otherwise the "{}display"{} flag}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1252 \textcolor{comment}{ * is used to determine whether to copy pixels that are not in the current pass.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1253 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1254 \textcolor{comment}{ * Because 'png\_do\_read\_interlace' (below) replicates pixels this allows this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1255 \textcolor{comment}{ * function to achieve the documented 'blocky' appearance during interlaced read}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1256 \textcolor{comment}{ * if display is 1 and the 'sparkle' appearance, where existing pixels in 'row'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1257 \textcolor{comment}{ * are not changed if they are not in the current pass, when display is 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1258 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1259 \textcolor{comment}{ * 'display' must be 0 or 1, otherwise the memcpy will be done regardless.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1260 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1261 \textcolor{comment}{ * The API always reads from the png\_struct row buffer and always assumes that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1262 \textcolor{comment}{ * it is full width (png\_do\_read\_interlace has already been called.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1263 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1264 \textcolor{comment}{ * This function is only ever used to write to row buffers provided by the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1265 \textcolor{comment}{ * caller of the relevant libpng API and the row must have already been}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1266 \textcolor{comment}{ * transformed by the read transformations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1267 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1268 \textcolor{comment}{ * The PNG\_USE\_COMPILE\_TIME\_MASKS option causes generation of pre-\/computed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1269 \textcolor{comment}{ * bitmasks for use within the code, otherwise runtime generated masks are used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1270 \textcolor{comment}{ * The default is compile time masks.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1271 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1272 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef PNG\_USE\_COMPILE\_TIME\_MASKS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1273 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#  define PNG\_USE\_COMPILE\_TIME\_MASKS 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1274 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1275 \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ab95ee9198d98980acb4cb4532f1e3637}{PNG\_INTERNAL\_FUNCTION}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void},\mbox{\hyperlink{pngrutil_8c_ae9eb8f26ea3376ed77b7d66fde8a9281}{png\_combine\_row}},(\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_ad21074dd8cb2466bcf2d187b29d3a91f}{png\_const\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}},}

\DoxyCodeLine{1802 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_BENIGN\_ERRORS\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803 \textcolor{comment}{/* Application errors (new in 1.6); use these functions (declared below) for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804 \textcolor{comment}{ * errors in the parameters or order of API function calls on read.  The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805 \textcolor{comment}{ * 'warning' should be used for an error that can be handled completely; the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806 \textcolor{comment}{ * 'error' for one which can be handled safely but which may lose application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807 \textcolor{comment}{ * information or settings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1808 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809 \textcolor{comment}{ * By default these both result in a png\_error call prior to release, while in a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810 \textcolor{comment}{ * released version the 'warning' is just a warning.  However if the application}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811 \textcolor{comment}{ * explicitly disables benign errors (explicitly permitting the code to lose}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812 \textcolor{comment}{ * information) they both turn into warnings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814 \textcolor{comment}{ * If benign errors aren't supported they end up as the corresponding base call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815 \textcolor{comment}{ * (png\_warning or png\_error.)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1835    \textcolor{comment}{/* Report a recoverable issue in chunk data.  On read this is used to report}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1846 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_CHUNK\_ERROR       2 }\textcolor{comment}{/* always an error */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1848 \textcolor{comment}{/* ASCII to FP interfaces, currently only implemented if sCAL}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1858 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1859 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FLOATING\_POINT\_SUPPORTED}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1865 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef PNG\_FIXED\_POINT\_SUPPORTED}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866 \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ab95ee9198d98980acb4cb4532f1e3637}{PNG\_INTERNAL\_FUNCTION}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void},\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8c_a7e76c9e3e01a91efdc30745ca87ea6f3}{png\_ascii\_from\_fixed}},(\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_ad21074dd8cb2466bcf2d187b29d3a91f}{png\_const\_structrp}} \mbox{\hyperlink{png_8h_a35dc82857793b55e7c8bb6f32f8ca764}{png\_ptr}},}

\DoxyCodeLine{1868 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* FIXED\_POINT */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* sCAL */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1871 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(PNG\_sCAL\_SUPPORTED) || defined(PNG\_pCAL\_SUPPORTED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1872 \textcolor{comment}{/* An internal API to validate the format of a floating point number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1873 \textcolor{comment}{ * The result is the index of the next character.  If the number is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874 \textcolor{comment}{ * not valid it will be the index of a character in the supposed number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876 \textcolor{comment}{ * The format of a number is defined in the PNG extensions specification}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 \textcolor{comment}{ * and this API is strictly conformant to that spec, not anyone elses!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1878 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879 \textcolor{comment}{ * The format as a regular expression is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881 \textcolor{comment}{ * [+-\/]?[0-\/9]+.?([Ee][+-\/]?[0-\/9]+)?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883 \textcolor{comment}{ * or:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885 \textcolor{comment}{ * [+-\/]?.[0-\/9]+(.[0-\/9]+)?([Ee][+-\/]?[0-\/9]+)?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1886 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887 \textcolor{comment}{ * The complexity is that either integer or fraction must be present and the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1888 \textcolor{comment}{ * fraction is permitted to have no digits only if the integer is present.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890 \textcolor{comment}{ * NOTE: The dangling E problem.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891 \textcolor{comment}{ *   There is a PNG valid floating point number in the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893 \textcolor{comment}{ *       PNG floating point numbers are not greedy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895 \textcolor{comment}{ *   Working this out requires *TWO* character lookahead (because of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896 \textcolor{comment}{ *   sign), the parser does not do this -\/ it will fail at the 'r' -\/ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897 \textcolor{comment}{ *   doesn't matter for PNG sCAL chunk values, but it requires more care}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898 \textcolor{comment}{ *   if the value were ever to be embedded in something more complex.  Use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899 \textcolor{comment}{ *   ANSI-\/C strtod if you need the lookahead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901 \textcolor{comment}{/* State table for the parser. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_INTEGER    0  }\textcolor{comment}{/* before or in integer */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_FRACTION   1  }\textcolor{comment}{/* before or in fraction */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1904 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_EXPONENT   2  }\textcolor{comment}{/* before or in exponent */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_STATE      3  }\textcolor{comment}{/* mask for the above */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_SAW\_SIGN   4  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Saw +/-\/ in current state */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1907 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT  8  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Saw a digit in current state */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DOT   16  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Saw a dot in current state */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_SAW\_E     32  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Saw an E (or e) in current state */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1910 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_SAW\_ANY   60  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Saw any of the above 4 */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1912 \textcolor{comment}{/* These three values don't affect the parser.  They are set but not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1913 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1914 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_WAS\_VALID 64  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Preceding substring is a valid fp number */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1915 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_NEGATIVE 128  }\textcolor{comment}{/* A negative number, including "{}-\/0"{} */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1916 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_NONZERO  256  }\textcolor{comment}{/* A non-\/zero value */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1917 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_STICKY   448  }\textcolor{comment}{/* The above three flags */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1918 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1919 \textcolor{comment}{/* This is available for the caller to store in 'state' if required.  Do not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1920 \textcolor{comment}{ * call the parser after setting it (the parser sometimes clears it.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1921 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1922 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_INVALID  512  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Available for callers as a distinct value */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1923 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1924 \textcolor{comment}{/* Result codes for the parser (boolean -\/ true meants ok, false means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1925 \textcolor{comment}{ * not ok yet.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1926 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1927 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_MAYBE      0  }\textcolor{comment}{/* The number may be valid in the future */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1928 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_OK         1  }\textcolor{comment}{/* The number is valid */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1929 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1930 \textcolor{comment}{/* Tests on the sticky non-\/zero and negative flags.  To pass these checks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1931 \textcolor{comment}{ * the state must also indicate that the whole number is valid -\/ this is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1932 \textcolor{comment}{ * achieved by testing PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT (see the implementation for why this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1933 \textcolor{comment}{ * is equivalent to PNG\_FP\_OK above.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1934 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1935 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_NZ\_MASK (PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT | PNG\_FP\_NEGATIVE | PNG\_FP\_NONZERO)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1936    \textcolor{comment}{/* NZ\_MASK: the string is valid and a non-\/zero negative value */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1937 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_Z\_MASK (PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT | PNG\_FP\_NONZERO)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1938    \textcolor{comment}{/* Z MASK: the string is valid and a non-\/zero value. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1939    \textcolor{comment}{/* PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT: the string is valid. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1940 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_IS\_ZERO(state) (((state) \& PNG\_FP\_Z\_MASK) == PNG\_FP\_SAW\_DIGIT)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1941 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_IS\_POSITIVE(state) (((state) \& PNG\_FP\_NZ\_MASK) == PNG\_FP\_Z\_MASK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1942 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define PNG\_FP\_IS\_NEGATIVE(state) (((state) \& PNG\_FP\_NZ\_MASK) == PNG\_FP\_NZ\_MASK)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1943 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1944 \textcolor{comment}{/* The actual parser.  This can be called repeatedly. It updates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1945 \textcolor{comment}{ * the index into the string and the state variable (which must}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1946 \textcolor{comment}{ * be initialized to 0).  It returns a result code, as above.  There}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1947 \textcolor{comment}{ * is no point calling the parser any more if it fails to advance to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1948 \textcolor{comment}{ * the end of the string -\/ it is stuck on an invalid character (or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1949 \textcolor{comment}{ * terminated by '\(\backslash\)0').}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1950 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1951 \textcolor{comment}{ * Note that the pointer will consume an E or even an E+ and then leave}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1952 \textcolor{comment}{ * a 'maybe' state even though a preceding integer.fraction is valid.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1953 \textcolor{comment}{ * The PNG\_FP\_WAS\_VALID flag indicates that a preceding substring was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1954 \textcolor{comment}{ * a valid number.  It's possible to recover from this by calling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1955 \textcolor{comment}{ * the parser again (from the start, with state 0) but with a string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1956 \textcolor{comment}{ * that omits the last character (i.e. set the size to the index of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1957 \textcolor{comment}{ * the problem character.)  This has not been tested within libpng.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1958 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1959 \mbox{\hyperlink{pngpriv_8h_ab95ee9198d98980acb4cb4532f1e3637}{PNG\_INTERNAL\_FUNCTION}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int},\mbox{\hyperlink{png_8c_a5a98f5a8957b9b68d04a3f1ca5885ad2}{png\_check\_fp\_number}},(\mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_adee13ff9d091a8ae795d650a4be82b80}{png\_const\_charp}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{string},}
\DoxyCodeLine{1960    \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegl_a441d79156826d7dfbf89100bb934a38d}{size}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *statep, \mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a226c996cee25679a0b1f340f7946040e}{png\_size\_tp}} whereami),\mbox{\hyperlink{pngconf_8h_a6501ad1ed16700c401830c9001c6768f}{PNG\_EMPTY}});}
